#    DataFrame   .
def number_encode_features(init_df):
    result = init_df.copy() #    
    encoders = {}
    for column in result.columns:
        if result.dtypes[column] == object: # np.object --   /    - ,    
            encoders[column] = preprocessing.LabelEncoder() #   column  
            result[column] = encoders[column].fit_transform(result[column]) #       
    return result, encoders

encoded_data, encoders = number_encode_features(df) #  encoded data   .
